<P_I,38>

{ED:46._THOMAS_STONOR_TO_[SIR_JOHN_FORTESCUE]}

{ED:30_October,_1424}

<P_I,39>

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Ryth welle belovyd syr , I grete yow well , doyng yow to undurstonde
+tath yowre son Jon and I beth fully acorded as towchyng to the ferme
of the Maner off Ermyngton , as hys endenturys +terof beth enseylyd .
STONOR,I,39.001.1

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
And ye shall have +te lawe Court of Mychellmasse last passed .
STONOR,I,39.001.2

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Fur+turmore I send yow be the berer of +tys letter endenturys betwene
yowre sone Rychard and my feffeys , +te wyche ben made be avyse and
asent of yowre son Jon : prayinge yow that ye delyver nat the party of
+te same endenturys enselyd be my feffeys into the tyme that yowre sone
Rychard have enselyd hys party of the same endenturys : and thanne hys
party soo enselyd that ye delyver sesyng unto the same Rychard and hys
wyff aftyr the fourme of the endenturys : to wyche endenturys lakketh
+te selyng of my uncle Belknap , wyche shall ensele +tem whanne he com
fro beyonde see . STONOR,I,39.001.3

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
And seeth that yowre forseyde son Rychard duly ensele +te same
endenture , STONOR,I,39.001.4

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
for yowre son Jonys honestie hanketh theron . STONOR,I,39.001.5

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
And as towchyng the warde of Wytburyes heyr , and of +te londys , the
wyche longen to me , I pray yow that ye soo see +terto that my ryth be
saved , that I and my frendus schull have yow thonke therfore . And yf
ye see that hyt may lawfully be sesyd +tath ye sesed
{ED:hyt_AFTERWARDS_ERASED} as my trust ys in yow . STONOR,I,39.001.6

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Nomore y wryte unto yow at thys tyme , but the holy gost have yow in
hys kepyng . STONOR,I,39.001.7

AUTHOR:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:31?
RECIPIENT:JOHN_FORTESCUE:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_001:M3:1424:UNKNOWN:OTHER
I-wrytte at London the Monday nexte before alle-halwenday . By Thomas
Stonore . STONOR,I,39.001.8

{ED:NO_ENDORSEMENT.}

<P_I,47>

{ED:53._ALYS,_LADY_SUDELEY_TO_THOMAS_STONOR}

{ED:before_1431}

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Right trusty and entierly welbeloved frend y commaund me unto you :
STONOR,I,47.002.9

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and , where as y of singler trust in you have before this enfeffed you
with other in my Maners , londes and tenements withyn dyvers shires ,
wole and hertely prey you , for gret consideracions and causes touching
my worship and gret profyt , that ye seale the deedes , made yn youre
name and other , of the seid Maners to suche persons as be named in the
same , wheche seid deedes the berer of this shall shewe unto you , as
my full trust ys and hathe be unto you , like as the berer hereof shall
enfourme you : to whom y prey you geve credence . STONOR,I,47.002.10

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
And , sir , yf ther be anything that y may do for you in any mater in
tyme comyng , y wole do yt with all myn hert , STONOR,I,47.002.11

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and that knoweth God , who have you in his blessed kepyng .
STONOR,I,47.002.12

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Wreten at Sudely the iiij day of Avrell . STONOR,I,47.002.13

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Alys , lady Sudeley . STONOR,I,47.002.14

AUTHOR:ALICE_SUDELEY:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_I:MALE:_:1393?:_
LETTER:STONOR_002:M3:1420S?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
To the worshipfull and my trusty frend Thomas Stoner .
STONOR,I,47.002.15

<P_I,55>

{ED:63._JOHN_FRENDE_TO_THOMAS_STONOR}

{ED:?_April,_1462}

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Right worshipfull maister , I comaunde me unto yov : praying yov to
sende me word by your letter where ye wil come in to Devenshire to
abide other no &c : and what I shall do with the corne , syder , and
wyne : STONOR,I,55.003.16

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
yf ye come nought , hit were best , me semeth , that hit were sold
betyme &c . STONOR,I,55.003.17

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Also tenentes of Modbury , that is to sey John Torryng <P_I,56> and
other , have made an ende with Ric. Fortescu in your defaute ,
understondyng to them that ye wold have come , and kepe not your
promise at no tyme &c . STONOR,I,56.003.18

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Item , waen Ric. Fortescu was there in lente nov last past he sende to
Modbury by John Saunder seyng , that he hadde recoveryd of Thomas
Stonore a C. li : STONOR,I,56.003.19

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
and wel a wist they schuld be cast in suche daunger as they schuld
never abere : STONOR,I,56.003.20

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
and for fere of suche langage the seid Torryng and other have made
there ende under this condicion , what they schall paie , though &c hit
passe ayenst them . STONOR,I,56.003.21

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Item , the mede I kepe in your honde unto tyme ye sende me word what I
schall do . STONOR,I,56.003.22

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Item , I do yov to wete that my maister Drayton hath sende me word that
I schulde fylle a grete parte of the Southwode : STONOR,I,56.003.23

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
I pray yov sende me word where hit be your will or noo .
STONOR,I,56.003.24

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_003:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT

<P_I,56>

{ED:64._JOHN_FRENDE_TO_THOMAS_STONOR}

{ED:c._1462}

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Right worshipfull maister , I recomaunde me unto yov : letyng yov wete
that Thomas Baron , John Peperell , the son of Robert Peperell ,
mauneseth me dayly , and put me in suche fere of my lyffe , that with
other the servauntes of Ric. Fortescu , that I dere not go to cherche
ne <P_I,57> to chepyng . STONOR,I,57.004.27

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Also now late the seid Baron and Peperell have sklaunder me that I
schuld sende divers men to the hous of the seid Thomas ; and ther and
at that tyme the seid persons , that is to wete John Gune , John
Cleveff and other , schuld take theefly xxvj. s. viij. d. of the godis
of the seid John Peperell , vj spones of silver of the godis of Thomas
Barons , and a girdell with silver harnes of his susters , and divers
polen , and brynge althis to the hous of John Frende of Ermyngton : and
there and at that tyme then schuld recette : uppon the whiche sklaunder
and untrue noyse the seid John Frende hath made his purge with meny
worshippfull gentilmen and gode yoman . Wherefore I pray yov that ye
see a meane that I may be in ese : STONOR,I,57.004.28

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
for hit is worse than ever hit was : STONOR,I,57.004.29

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
for ye have seid many tymes that ye wold come thether , and dwelle ther
: STONOR,I,57.004.30

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
and that thay putteth in uterance daily that we $shall $be
{TEXT:schalbe} undowe , STONOR,I,57.004.31

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
for ye nel never come to helpe us . STONOR,I,57.004.32

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Also I pray yov that my maister Drayton may se this letter , and be
enformyd thereof . STONOR,I,57.004.33

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT

Thomas Baron . STONOR,I,57.004.34

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT

ayenst me . STONOR,I,57.004.35

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT

STONOR,I,57.004.36

AUTHOR:JOHN_FRENDE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_004:M4:1462:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
for I may not STONOR,I,57.004.37

{ED:65._THOMAS_HAMPTON_TO_THOMAS_STONOR}

{ED:1462}

<P_I,58>

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_005:M4:1462:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Rytht wurschypfull and my tender welbelovyd Cosyn , I recommaunde me to
yow : letyng yow wyte +tat my Suster Swete recommaundyth her to yow ,
and hertyly thankyth yow for her chylderyn , STONOR,I,58.005.42

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_005:M4:1462:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and so do I as well for owr venyson . STONOR,I,58.005.43

RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:38
LETTER:STONOR_005:M4:1462:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Syr , sche prayth yow specyally to make your effectuell labor $unto the
parson of Sylverton +tat he wull in weye of Crystes charyte loke up all
suche evydens as in eny wyse may make eny proffe Thomas to be +te son
of Syr Water and Jahne his ffurst wyff . STONOR,I,58.005.44

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_

<P_I,104>

{ED:100._THOMAS_MULL_TO_THOMAS_STONOR}

{ED:[1469]}

<P_I,105>

AUTHOR:THOMAS_MULL:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:45?
LETTER:STONOR_016:M4:1469?:UNKNOWN:FAMILY_SERVANT
Right worshipfull Master and Brother , I recommaund me unto you :
prayng you to conceyve that or Robert Barre come I had borowed iij. li.
to content and paye Rayne of Devonshir for your offis upon the diem
clausit extremum after the dethe of my good Mastres and Moder and your
, whos sowle God assoyle , which I have payd hym . STONOR,I,105.016.241

AUTHOR:THOMAS_MULL:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:45?
LETTER:STONOR_016:M4:1469?:UNKNOWN:FAMILY_SERVANT
And syr , I conceyve by Robert ye wold I shold make up the offis
accordyng to suche instruccion as ye sent by hym to my cosyn Willyam in
a bille , which I dar not take uppon me , for I conceyve it not a right
: wherefor I pray you to come your self and to bryng with you the cope
of all thos dedes : STONOR,I,105.016.242

AUTHOR:THOMAS_MULL:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:45?
LETTER:STONOR_016:M4:1469?:UNKNOWN:FAMILY_SERVANT
or ell , and ye be not disposid to come here this terme , send us a
pleyn cope of al your dedes made seth the dethe of your ffader with a
more playne instruccion , STONOR,I,105.016.243

By the King . STONOR,I,115.019.297

Edw . STONOR,I,115.019.298

AUTHOR:EDWARD_IV:MALE:_:1442:28
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:46
LETTER:STONOR_019:M4:1470:COPY:OTHER
Trusty and welebeloved We grete you wele ; Letting you wit +tat our
Traitours and Rebelles +te Duc of Clarence and Therl of Warrewik ,
<P_I,116> which daily labour +te weyes moyens at +teir power of our
final destruccion , and +te subversion of this owre Realme and +te
comon wele of +te same , been fledde westwardes : Whome we wol folowe
and pursue with our Ooste with al diligence possible , and let and
represse +teir fals and traiteroux purpose and entent with Goddes grace
. Wherfore we wol and straitely charge you +tat immediatly after +te
sight of +ties owre lettres ye arredie you , with such a fellasship on
horssebak in defensible arraye as ye goodly can make , to come unto us
wheresoever ye shal undrestande +tat we +ten $shall $be {TEXT:shalbee}
, to aide and assiste us to thentent aforesaid , without failling as ye
love and tendre the wele of us and of owre said Realme , and uppon the
feith and liegeaunce that ye owe unto us . STONOR,I,116.019.299

AUTHOR:EDWARD_IV:MALE:_:1442:28
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:46
LETTER:STONOR_019:M4:1470:COPY:OTHER
Yoven undre owre Signet at owre Citie of Coventre , +te iij=de= day of
Aprill . STONOR,I,116.019.300

AUTHOR:EDWARD_IV:MALE:_:1442:28
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:46
LETTER:STONOR_019:M4:1470:COPY:OTHER
To our trusty and welebeloved Thomas Stoner of Stoner .
STONOR,I,116.019.301

{ED:17_January_[1471?]}

AUTHOR:WADEHILL:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:47?
LETTER:STONOR_020:M4:1471?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Worshipfull and my right good maister , I recommende me to youre good
maistership : STONOR,I,116.020.302

AUTHOR:WADEHILL:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:47?
LETTER:STONOR_020:M4:1471?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
and like you wete +tat my lord , and my lady his Moder also , have
commaunded me to wryte unto you +tat +tey bothe hertily desire and prey
you , yef ye may in eny wyse or your goyng to London , ye wole take +te
laboure as to come hider to speke <P_I,117> with my seid lord and lady
for diverse grete matters and causes +tat +tey wolde speke unto you of
. STONOR,I,117.020.303

AUTHOR:WADEHILL:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:47?
LETTER:STONOR_020:M4:1471?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
And yef ye may not come hider , +tan +tat ye wole find +te meane to my
lord Chaunceler as to excuse my lord of his comyng not to London at
+tis time , like as my seid lord was wreten unto by a pryve seall
whiche was delivered to him on Munday last passed at vj of +te clokke
withynne night at Ewelme , which as your maystership knoweth well was
right shorte warnyng , remembring +tat +te more parte of my lordes
servauntes were sente into Suffolk to +te houshold +tere ayens
Crystemasse , and +te remenaunt of his servauntes , +tat were here
awayting , your maystership knoweth well been forthe with my lady , my
lordes wyf , into Suffolk to bringe her +tider : STONOR,I,117.020.304

AUTHOR:WADEHILL:MALE:_:_:_?

ladies here childerne , +tat been +tere . STONOR,I,117.020.305

{ED:125._DAME_KATHERINE_ARUNDELL_TO_THOMAS_STONOR}

{ED:7_Jan_[?_1473]}

<P_I,129>

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Ryght trusty Cosyn , I comaunde me to you : STONOR,I,129.027.439

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and where as hit was agreed by you and my councell at your beyng at
Dorchester byfore Crystmasse that Richard Tomyowe , consyderyng the
gode service that he hath don for my husbonde and me in dayes passed
and the charges that he must do for me here after , shulde be made sure
of landes and tenementez to the yerely value of xx=ti= marke .
STONOR,I,129.027.440

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
And he ys agreed to take too lytill Manours in Corunwall , one called
Wynnyanton and the other called Kenell , of the value by the yere of
xij. li. : of the whiche I pray you , Cosyn , to speke to my cosyn Syr
Richard Harecourte and Edward Grymston that betweene you to sealle hym
a dede that William Menwynnek other Richard Reynolds shall brynge you
of the said Maners terme of his lyve : STONOR,I,129.027.441

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
for he woll not procede no furder in my maters in to the tyme he be
made sure of the same , whiche were to me a grete hurt , as ye
understonde . STONOR,I,129.027.442

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
And that this be done as my speciall trust is in you :
STONOR,I,129.027.443

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and our lorde have you in his blessed kepyng . STONOR,I,129.027.444

AUTHOR:KATHERINE_ARUNDELL:FEMALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:THOMAS_STONOR_II:MALE:_:1424:49?
LETTER:STONOR_027:M4:1473?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Wrytten at Excestre the xxvij=th= day off Janyver . By your Cosyn Dame
Kateryne Arundell . STONOR,I,129.027.445

offycers there that ther may no ffyssch com up : wherfore the gentelmen
that holdyth the water may not paye ther rente , and as thay havyth
y-warnyd Water Frende . Wherapon y went to Willyam Fowel , as +ge
commandyt me , to wete what aunswer he had of Johne Gybbes :

as I do now , marvellyng grettly +tat ye be longe hense , remembryng
how grettely in consette ye stonde in London with a gentylwoman , and
the grette labore +tat hys made for here agynes you :

<P_I,154>

{ED:148._ALICE,_DUCHESS_OF_SUFFOLK_TO_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:5_March,_[?_1475]}

AUTHOR:ALICE_DE_LA_POLE:FEMALE:KIN:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:KIN:1449?:26?
LETTER:STONOR_034:M4:1475?:UNKNOWN:FAMILY_OTHER
Right trusty and entierly beloved ffrende we grete you well , desiryng
and praying yow , all excuses layde apart , that incontinent this
lettur seyne ye come to us to Ewelme for certayne grete causes
concernyng our wele and pleasir , whiche at your comyng ye shall
undrestond more pleynely : and theruppon ye to departe ayen at your
pleasir , so that ye fayle not here ynne at this tyme as our parfait
trust ys in you : and as in gretter case we woll be gladde to do for
you , that knoweth our lorde , who have you ever yn gouvernaunce .
STONOR,I,154.034.548

my ffadyr and a cowpyll off coneys : STONOR,II,14.049.821

{ED:185._THOMAS_BETSON_TO_DAME_ELIZABETH_STONOR}

{ED:22_Dec._[1477]}

AUTHOR:THOMAS_BETSON:MALE:SON_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:MOTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_054:M4:1477:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
Jhesu STONOR,II,27.054.976

AUTHOR:THOMAS_BETSON:MALE:SON_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:MOTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_054:M4:1477:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
Ano . STONOR,II,27.054.977

AUTHOR:THOMAS_BETSON:MALE:SON_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:MOTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_054:M4:1477:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
My most synguler good lady , after all dew commendacion hadd : please
it your good ladishipe to wete that I am throw and agreyd with Laurence
Fyncham , and have sett hym such surte as with the same he is right
well pleased . Whereffore , good madame , I beseche you to remembre myn
obligacion , the which ye have off myn , STONOR,II,27.054.978

{ED:199._JOHN,_ABBOT_OF_NORTON_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:[after_1477]}

AUTHOR:JOHN_OF_NORTON:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:_
LETTER:STONOR_061:M4:1470S:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Ryght wurschypfull and my fulgud Mayster after all due recommendacion
to yowe hade : prayng yowe to send me now in my grete necessite by the
berer heroff , my servant , your ferme ffor the parsonage of Pyrton ,
the whyche was due to have ben payd the viij day after the nativitie of
Saynt John Baptist : wher I had grett mervayll when my brothyr Schanon
no mone had so long taryyng in London over your promyse , me to grette
coste and hym to grett labur : STONOR,II,37.061.1061

AUTHOR:JOHN_OF_NORTON:MALE:_:_:_

for truly I had never gretter mestur then I nowe have , as my sayd

yow gyfe credens , STONOR,II,37.061.1065

{ED:213._GODARD_OXBRYGE_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:21_May,_1478}

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
Right onerabulle and worschipefull sir , and myn aspesyalle good
maister , I rekomend me unto your good mastershipe in the moste lowely
wise that {in}_P I beste can : sertefyinge your mastershepe that I ame
informyd by master Betson that Dave Wrykesame hathe reportyd sarten
langage by me in presens of my lady and on of her brodiryn :
STONOR,II,49.066.1167

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
and that is thus , STONOR,II,49.066.1168

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
that the seyd Daveht shold saye , that I told heme that maister Betson
schold tell me that he laboryd to your maistership and to my lady to
brynge the seyd Davyht owte of your conseythe and favore : the whyche I
take god to rekord that I never at no sesun repordid enny shyche wordys
to the seyd Davethe , nor to nonodir person , STONOR,II,49.066.1169

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
and that wyll I jostyfy as largely as enny trewe person owythe for to
jostyfy for a trowthe . STONOR,II,49.066.1170

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
And wan Mayster Betson told me of thys langege that Dawyth repordyd by
me , it came to my remembranse that Daveth hathe sayd to me that
maister Betson at Ester was a twelmonthe was srevyn off hys goostly
fadir , and that it was geven heme in penanse that he shold aske the
seyd Davyth forgevenes of this that maister Betson schold make labor to
your mastershipe to brynge the seyd Daveth owte of your conseyt and
favore . STONOR,II,49.066.1171

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
And fardirmore , the seyd Davythe sayd to me that maister Betson kowd
nat have absolysyon of hys goostly fadir tyll he had promysyd to brynge
the sayd Dave in your favor as myche as he was before .
STONOR,II,49.066.1172

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT
And thys seyd words Davyth hathe sayd to me , the whyche maister Betson
kene tell you more klerly by myn enformemasyon . STONOR,II,49.066.1173

AUTHOR:GODDARD_OXBRYGE:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_066:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_SERVANT

moneye the whyche is dewe to me by your maistershepe :
STONOR,II,49.066.1174

whiche ffor sothe I am right sory . STONOR,II,53.067.1190

loffyngest wyse +tat {in}_P my hart can thynnke , be my trouth :
thankynge your maystershipe right hartely off your curtesse and
loffynge letter , the which I have resseyvid by my M. your brodyr John
Croke . STONOR,II,56.068.1226

lady your wiffe and to all o+ter &c. : STONOR,II,56.068.1227

Est of Wycombe , for whiche y kepe the writ in my handes till unto the
tyme y understond what y shall do and how y $shall $be {TEXT:shalbe}

{ED:1_August,_1478}

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Jhesu . STONOR,II,65.073.1347

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
An=o=. xviij STONOR,II,65.073.1348

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Right Reverent and worschypfull lady , I recomaunde me unto your goode
ladyschyp , evermore desyring ffor to her off your goode wellfare , the
wyche I besche Jhesu longe to continue unto your hartys desyre &c .
STONOR,II,65.073.1349

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Fordermore , lady , ye schalle understonde that I have sent downe by
William Somer , bargemane of London , your beme and ij calys , the
<P_II,66> wyche I wrothe a bylle unto William Platys off that he
schulde resayve yt at Hendelay and so conevay yt unto Stonor .
STONOR,II,66.073.1350

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Fordermore , lady , ye schalle understonde that maysterys Hane , your
dowter , ys all moste hole , thankyd by Jhesu , STONOR,II,66.073.1351

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
and sche hys very mery . STONOR,II,66.073.1352

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
All so , lady , I beseke your goode ladyschype that I mythe have
cnowlage whedir that ye wollede have hany bere or hale , that I schulde
take in ayenst your comyng home unto London . STONOR,II,66.073.1353

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
No more unto your ladyschype at thys tyme but Jhesu have you in hys
kepyng . STONOR,II,66.073.1354

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Wretyn at London the ffyrst day of Agust . By your prentes Thomas
Henham . STONOR,II,66.073.1355

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Unto my Ryght Reverent and Worschypfull dame Elysabeth Stonor thys
letter be delyvered in hast , STONOR,II,66.073.1356

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HENHAM:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_
RECIPIENT:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_073:M4:1478:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
dd . STONOR,II,66.073.1357

{ED:226._DAME_ELIZABETH_STONOR_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:21_August,_1478}

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Jhesus . STONOR,II,66.074.1358

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Ryght enterly and my moste specyall belovyd husband , I recomaunde me
to yow yn the moste harty wyse , desyryng to here of yowre welefare &c.
, thankyng yow of yowre lettyr and of yowre partrechys .
STONOR,II,66.074.1359

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
And for Robert Warner , he ys cum to towne : STONOR,II,66.074.1360

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
dyverce of yowre servantys and myne have spoken with hym :
STONOR,II,66.074.1361

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
he seyeth that he can receyve no money as yet , notwithstondyng he
yntendyth to speke with me or he departe , and wyll content me yef he
may . STONOR,II,66.074.1362

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
I pray God that he may so do . STONOR,II,66.074.1363

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Also I pray yow to send me a answere of the mater that I wrote to yow
for the Lumbarde . STONOR,II,66.074.1364

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
And yef hyt myght plese yow to take the labur to ryde ovyr , then ye
may answere to the mater yowre selfe , whyche wyll be to me grete
hartes ese and plesure : STONOR,II,66.074.1365

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
for I thynke hyt ryght longe syth I speke with yow .
STONOR,II,66.074.1366

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Syr , I truste to Jhesu to se yow here yn shorte <P_II,67> tyme .
STONOR,II,67.074.1367

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
No more to yow at thys tyme , $but Jhesu preserve yow yn hys kepyng .
STONOR,II,67.074.1368

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
Wrytyn at Lundun the Fryday afore sent Bartylmewys day . By your owne
wyff Elysabeth Stonore . STONOR,II,67.074.1369

AUTHOR:ELIZABETH_STONOR[N.CROKE]:FEMALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_074:M4:1478:COPY:FAMILY_NUCLEAR
To my most enterly belovyd husband Syr Wylliam Stonore , knyght .
STONOR,II,67.074.1370

<P_II,70>

{ED:231._HENRY_DOGETT_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:24_Dec._[?_1478]}

AUTHOR:HENRY_DOGETT:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_076:M4:1478?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Ryght worshepfull and my goode and feithfull maister , after dew
recomendacion pleasith yow to wete +tat my clerke and your servaunte
have been at Abendon with the vicar of Seynt Elyns to have leverey of
your cuppe , and offurred hym x. li. acordyng to your writeyng :
STONOR,II,70.076.1406

AUTHOR:HENRY_DOGETT:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_076:M4:1478?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
and he <P_II,71> answered them that he wold not deliver the said cuppe
with owte the bille indented +tat is made bytwene yow be brought upon
the deliveraunce : and to have sewrete for the residew of the money to
be paid at Candelmas next . STONOR,II,71.076.1407

AUTHOR:HENRY_DOGETT:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_076:M4:1478?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
I remitte all to your maistershep and wysedome . STONOR,II,71.076.1408

AUTHOR:HENRY_DOGETT:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_076:M4:1478?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
The said x. li. shall be redy at eny tyme that ye like , havyng fro
your maistershep a writeyng to be content ayen by Ester next comynge .
STONOR,II,71.076.1409

AUTHOR:HENRY_DOGETT:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_076:M4:1478?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
And God preserve yow , my good lady , your wyfe , and all yours .
STONOR,II,71.076.1410

AUTHOR:HENRY_DOGETT:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:29?
LETTER:STONOR_076:M4:1478?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
At Aston , a Cristemas yeve with the hand of your servaunt Henry Dogett

{ED:236._THOMAS_HAMPTON_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:2_Jan._[?_1479]}

<P_II,76>

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Ryht worshypfull and feythfully lovyng Cosyn , I recomaunde unto you .
STONOR,II,76.078.1428

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Syr , I was enformed by my sone Froste that hit lyked you upon
cominicacon had between you and Waller that ye lete hym understonde in
brefe termes , yef hym lyked the mariage betwen your kynneswoman and
hym , that he shold make hyr joyntour of xx=ti=. li. worth londe
acordyng to hys owne promyse , STONOR,II,76.078.1429

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and elles ye lete hym understonde he shold no ferther enter in
cominicacon in the mater : STONOR,II,76.078.1430

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
and when he understode your decre and jugement , he was therto agreable
. STONOR,II,76.078.1431

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Syr , I understonde he entendeth to be with me in ij days after the
xij=th= day . STONOR,II,76.078.1432

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Syr , me thoght by informacion of my sone Froste that he entendeth in
most hasty wyse to be maried : wherfor me semyth , savyng your better
advyse , that hit ys me to desyre of hym to be bounden and sum persons
with hym , that he shall be Ester day then next folowyng do make hyr
suer of hyr joyntour . STONOR,II,76.078.1433

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?
LETTER:STONOR_078:M4:1479?:UNKNOWN:OTHER
Syr , that hit may plese you to lemyte me in what sum I may desyr them
to be bounden yn , I pray send me word by my servaunt , the brynger of
thys letter , and how longe ye entend to be aboute home efter the
xij=th= tyde . STONOR,II,76.078.1434

AUTHOR:THOMAS_HAMPTON:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:30?

And good syr , that thys my sympyll wrytyng may recommaund me to my
good Cosyn , my lady your wyfe , STONOR,II,76.078.1435

all hir place : the which woman hase ben in pesibill possession thes

mighty Godde to preserve you to youre most pleasure and hertis desire .

acounte wyth the sayde Scherve off the mercement wythyn your hunderd

hunderd : STONOR,II,107.090.1608

to the hole stokke of your ij chyldryn , Hewe and Margarete :

{ED:285._RICHARD_GERMYN_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:7_April_[1481]}

AUTHOR:RICHARD_GERMYN:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_100:M4:1481?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Right Wurshipfull and Onerable Maister , y comaund me unto you with
alle suche servyse as {with}_P y can or may . STONOR,II,119.100.1748

AUTHOR:RICHARD_GERMYN:MALE:FAMILY_SERVANT:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_100:M4:1481?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Please your maistership have enknowliche here y sende the copy of a
writte , which is agayn you at the Kinge is sute in Devonshire uppon
the Deum claus. extr. , which was <P_II,120> taken before the Escaetour
. STONOR,II,120.100.1749

Also I moved you at my last being at Stonore that my lord Markas his
officer hath distrayned your tenaunt at Clist , and clemyth a mersshe ,
the third ffote in alle the said mersshe , where as he nor noon of his
ancetours oute of tyme that no mynde is never had :
STONOR,II,120.100.1753

seid mersshe shuld ly voyde and not to be ocupyed in to the tyme that
my lorde and ye hadde spoken together : STONOR,II,120.100.1754

{ED:286._RICHARD_SALTER_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:11_April_[1481]}

AUTHOR:RICHARD_SALTER:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_101:M4:1481:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Ryght worshypfull Syr , and my specyall good master , I commaunde me to
yow STONOR,II,121.101.1805

AUTHOR:RICHARD_SALTER:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_101:M4:1481:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
and where hyt ys so as I am enformyd +tat on doctor Eggecombe , late
resydencyare of Exeter , is decesyd , +te whyche hadde a benefyce
callyd Ermynton in Devonshyre of your patronage , now beyng <P_II,122>
voyde , +te whyche I have harde reporte +ge entende to apropure or to
have lycence to make a chauntre or ij off , to +te whyche I am enformyd
+te bysshoppe woll in no wyse assent : wherfore yff +ge kan notte
opteyn your purpose , butte moste nedys gyff hytte , yff hytte wold
plese yow to have me rememburyd +terunto , I were ever bounden to be
your beddemann , and to pray for yow , as God knowyth , who ever
preserve yow , STONOR,II,122.101.1806

AUTHOR:RICHARD_SALTER:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_101:M4:1481:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Amen . STONOR,II,122.101.1807

RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?

Wryton in hast +te xj day of Aprile . STONOR,II,122.101.1808

RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_101:M4:1481:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
I pray yow geve credens to +te berer heroff . STONOR,II,122.101.1809

RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?

Your one to hys power , Richard Salter , doctor .
STONOR,II,122.101.1810

{ED:299._JOHN_SHYNNER_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:[c._1481]}

AUTHOR:JOHN_SHYNNER:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_108:M4:1481:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Most worchepfull and reveryend Mayster , I recummend me onto yowr
reverynd Maisterchep also lowly as I can hoder may : wyllyng yowr
Maysterchep to have knowleche +tat syr Wylyam Sandys ys gretely
dysplesyd with me , and Jaye do lesayd maner also , as for a grehowde
+tat I scholde send onto yowr maysterchep as they say : +te weche I
know not what coler +tis grehowd ys , noder no seche I send to yow ,
neyder was consente +ter to : werefor I beseche yowr maysterchep to
wrythe onto Syr Wiliam Sandys as for myne a skese , and to speke to
Jaye at Londun , wen , ye methe with hym , as my treste ys on yowr
Maysterchep , and as I schall and am yowr preste to praye to God for
yow and yowrys , ho have yow and yowrs in hys kepyng ever ,
STONOR,II,133.108.1918

AUTHOR:JOHN_SHYNNER:MALE:_:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?

your preste Syr John Shynner . STONOR,II,133.108.1920

{ED:300._JOHN_SHYNNER_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR}

{ED:[?_1481]}

AUTHOR:JOHN_SHYNNER:MALE:_:_:_?
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:_:1449?:32?
LETTER:STONOR_109:M4:1481?:AUTOGRAPH:OTHER
Ry+gth reverent and worcheppell Mayster , I recommende me on to yowr
Maysterchepp allso hertely as I can and may : prayeng yowr Maysterchepp

to +gour maistyrshyp at divers tymes in +te +gere , lyke as Mr.
Eadmunde , Mr. Flynte , Mr. Kyckall , and I with o+ter moye dyd layte ;
off whome I desyryd +te commyssare to inquire +gour worshypfull and

{ED:347._LETTER_OF_PRIVY_SEAL_TO_HUMPHREY_FORSTER_OTHERS.}


{ED:16_April_1471}

AUTHOR:EDWARD_IV:MALE:_:1442:29
RECIPIENT:HUMPHREY_FORSTER_&:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_127:M4:1471:COPY:OTHER_CODE_METADATA
By +t=e= Kyng . STONOR,III,10.127.2226

AUTHOR:EDWARD_IV:MALE:_:1442:29
RECIPIENT:HUMPHREY_FORSTER_&:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_127:M4:1471:COPY:OTHER_CODE_METADATA
Trusty and webelovid we grete you wel , latyng you wete +tat in our
Batel late had , whereof God of his grete grace hathe yeven us vyctory
, owre Rebelles and traytours , +t=e= Duke of Excetr. , +t=e= marquis
Montagu , +t=e= Erles of Warwyk and Oxinford with other ben slayne ,
and +t=e= remenaunt put to flyght , for +t=e= whiche we and alle oure
trew Subgettes owe to yeve laude and thonke to God of whom alle grace
cometh : Wherfor we desire and pray you as oure trew Subgettes to
thanke hym +terof , willyng also alle other to yeve unto hym lawdes and
thankes for +t=e= same : STONOR,III,10.127.2227

AUTHOR:EDWARD_IV:MALE:_:1442:29
RECIPIENT:HUMPHREY_FORSTER_&:MALE:_:_:_
LETTER:STONOR_127:M4:1471:COPY:OTHER_CODE_METADATA
And over this we woll +tat ye charge and commaunde on oure behalf alle
people of oure Countee of Oxinford and other places near ajoynyng to
+t=e= same of ye age of be twyxte lx=ti= and xvj=ne= yeres , hable to
do us servise to be redy in alle possible hast in +tere most defensible
araye and theym so arayde bryng unto us for +t=e= repressyng and
subdewyng of certeyn oure Rebelles enemyes and traytours , not failyng
herof us STONOR,III,10.127.2228

ye wol answere unto us at your peryl . STONOR,III,10.127.2229

<P_III,17>

{ED:355._HUMPHREY_FORSTER_TO_SIR_WILLIAM_STONOR.}

{ED:[c._1480.]}

AUTHOR:HUMPHREY_FORSTER:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:1449?:31?
LETTER:STONOR_129:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
Right worshipfull nevewe , in my most feythefull wyse I recommaunde me
to you . STONOR,III,17.129.2251

AUTHOR:HUMPHREY_FORSTER:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:1449?:31?
LETTER:STONOR_129:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
And pleaseth you to wete that one Robert Bolle , a tenaunt of myne of
Henle hath be with me and enformed me that his Brother dwellyng at
Rysborowe shuld be atached for a Scot by servauntes of yours , wher in
dede he is none , STONOR,III,17.129.2252

AUTHOR:HUMPHREY_FORSTER:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:1449?:31?
LETTER:STONOR_129:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
for he and his brother that is my servaunt were bore but ij myle from
syr James <em> Strangewysshes place </em> . whiche is fifty myle from
Scotlond and more . STONOR,III,17.129.2253

AUTHOR:HUMPHREY_FORSTER:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:1449?:31?
LETTER:STONOR_129:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
And his fader and moder $tenaunts to syr James Strangewissh , which
wolle be dewly proved : wherfore I beseche yow to showe your favorabill
maistership to them as conciens and ryght require .
STONOR,III,17.129.2254

AUTHOR:HUMPHREY_FORSTER:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:_:_
RECIPIENT:WILLIAM_STONOR:MALE:BROTHER_IN_LAW:1449?:31?
LETTER:STONOR_129:M4:1480:AUTOGRAPH:FAMILY_OTHER
And Jesu preserve yow . STONOR,III,17.129.2255

Wreten in hast this same Moneday . STONOR,III,17.129.2256

Thomas Raufe was with me this same Moneday in +t=e= mornyng , for
Poughlowe lond to understond what direccion Herre Doget wold abide :
STONOR,III,17.129.2257
